    <!-- Main hero unit for a primary marketing message or call to action --> 
    <div class="hero-unit"> 
     <p>The Office of the President is the systemwide headquarters of the University of California, managing its fiscal and business operations, and supporting the academic and research missions across its campuses, labs and medical centers.</p> 
     <p><a href="mission/index.html" title="UCOP mission">Learn more</a></p> 
    </div>

         <ul class="dropdown-menu sidebar-pop"> 
          <li> <h3>Academic Affairs</h3> <p>We are a systemwide resource for academic excellence in research, teaching and public service.</p> <p class="dept">Departments</p> 
           <ul> 
            <li><a href="/academic-personnel/index.html">Academic Personnel</a></li> 
            <li><a href="/academic-planning-programs-coordination/index.html">Academic Planning, Programs &amp; Coordination</a></li>

           </ul> </li> 
         </ul> </li>

         <ul class="dropdown-menu sidebar-pop">

       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span9"> 
         <h2>The President</h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="span3 pull-right socialbtns-rt"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span11"> 
         <blockquote>
          “The University of California is preeminent in educating the state’s young people, in enhancing research and scholarship in every discipline, in fostering economic growth, medicine, the arts, its athletic and other programs. Simply put, UC is the gold standard. Together, we must ensure that this standard is upheld.”
         </blockquote> 
         <p>Learn more about <a href="/president/index.html">President Janet Napolitano</a></p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div>

    <h2 class="long">Colleges, Divisions and Schools</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/academics/" title="Academics Home">Academics Home<br /><span>The backbone of the educational process</span></a></li>
       <li class="currentpage"><h3><dfn>Current page is: </dfn>Colleges, Divisions, and Schools</h3></li>
       <li><a href="/academics/undergradmajors.html" title="Undergraduate Programs">Undergraduate Programs<br /><span>Start your academic career here</span></a></li>
       <li><a href="/academics/gradprograms.html" title="Graduate Programs">Graduate Programs<br /><span>Take your education to the next level</span></a></li>
       <li><a href="http://www.extension.ucr.edu/" title="UCR Extension">UCR Extension<br /><span>Continue the learning experience</span></a></li>
       <li><a href="http://summer.ucr.edu/" title="Summer Sessions">Summer Sessions<br /><span>Get ahead in your education</span></a></li>
       <li><a href="/academics/resources.html" title="Student Resources">Student Resources<br /><span>Tools and information you need</span></a></li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
     <p> <a class="img_link" href="/dept.html" id="depts_button"> <span class="accessibility">Departments A to Z</span></a> </p> 
     <p><a id="ir_button" class="img_link" href="/international/"><span class="accessibility">International Resources.</span></a></p>

    <!-- End Sidebar --> 
    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <p><img src="/academics/images/collegesmall.jpg" alt="Students on campus." width="484" height="143" /> </p> 
     <h3>Taking Your Education Personally</h3> 
     <p>UC Riverside offers departments, colleges and degrees as dynamic and diverse as its student populace. Students and faculty work together to form a supportive learning environment that helps make a difference in the world through education and research.</p> 
     <p>UCR’s academic departments are organized into colleges, divisions and schools. Read on to learn more about each.</p> 
     <h3>Colleges</h3> 
     <p>There are three colleges at UCR, each encompassing wide-ranging subjects of study. These colleges are:</p> 
     <ul class="striped alt1"> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://www.engr.ucr.edu/">Bourns College of Engineering (BCOE)</a></strong><br />With a goal of producing engineers with the knowledge to serve rapidly changing technology and conducting cutting-edge research, the college stands as a catalyst for industrial growth in Inland Southern California, the state and the world.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://www.chass.ucr.edu/">College of Humanities, Arts, &amp; Social Sciences (CHASS)</a></strong><br />With a total of 20 different departments, the vast array of human experiences stands as the focus for CHASS. This unique combination of the arts, humanities, and social sciences creates an environment that fosters both creativity and learning.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://www.cnas.ucr.edu/">College of Natural &amp; Agricultural Sciences (CNAS)</a></strong><br />Thirteen different departments within three divisions covering the whole of physical, biological, mathematical and agricultural sciences make up this college. The university’s roots as a Citrus Experiment Station can be found within the college’s atmosphere of intimacy and excellence, diversity and distinction, and prestige and preeminence.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <h3>Schools</h3> 
     <p>UC Riverside has four stand-alone graduate/professional school programs.</p> 
     <ul class="striped alt1"> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://soba.ucr.edu/">School of Business Administration (SoBA)</a></strong><br />The school is made up of the <em><strong>A. Gary Anderson Graduate School of Management (AGSM) </strong></em>and the <em><strong>Undergraduate Business Program</strong></em>. AGSM is home to a full-time/part-time MBA program, an Executive MBA (EMBA) program, and a Ph.D. in business administration. The undergraduate program is the largest in the UC system and educates students in the art of science and management. Emphasis is placed upon students learning to work and compete in real-world business situations.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://www.education.ucr.edu/">Graduate School of Education (GSOE)</a></strong><br />A professional school responsible for linking research, instruction, and service in the field of education. GSOE faculty and students work with a number of programs designed to help educators at all levels take on today's toughest education challenges. Areas of emphasis include working more effectively with students with cognitive disorders, including autism.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://medschool.ucr.edu/">School of Medicine</a></strong><br /> This school will help meet the need for physicians in the medically underserved Inland Southern California region. The university's existing UCR/UCLA Thomas Haider Program in Biomedical Sciences has helped build a strong foundation for a medical school. When completed, the school will provide a pipeline for diversifying the physician workforce, facilitate partnerships with community clinics and hospitals, and develop new research and health care delivery programs.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://spp.ucr.edu">School of Public Policy</a></strong><br />For virtually every challenge facing growing communities worldwide, UCR is pioneering bold and practical solutions. Working in partnership with communities, policy makers, entrepreneurs, and business leaders in our own backyard and around the world, our School of Public Policy faculty and students bring fresh thinking to the complex challenges of poverty, crime, healthcare, education, pollution, water and energy security, immigration, sustainability, climate change and more.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <h3>Divisions</h3> 
     <p>Each of the university’s divisions is an independent, yet subordinate, administrative unit.</p> 
     <ul class="striped alt1"> 
      <li><strong>Division of Agriculture and Natural Resources</strong><br />Under the College of Natural and Agricultural Sciences, the division oversees the Departments of <a href="http://www.envisci.ucr.edu/">Environmental Sciences</a>, <a href="http://plantpath.ucr.edu/">Plant Pathology</a>, <a href="http://www.nematology.ucr.edu/">Nematology</a> and <a href="http://www.entomology.ucr.edu/">Entomology</a>.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://biomed.ucr.edu/">Division of Biomedical Sciences</a></strong><br />In conjunction with the David Geffen School of Medicine at UCLA, UCR students who have been enrolled in the program through the 2012-13 academic year complete their first two years of medical school at UCR and finish their M.D. degrees at UCLA. With the launch of UCR’s new medical school, applications are no longer being accepted for the UCR/UCLA Thomas Haider Program in Biomedical Sciences. <a href="http://medschool.ucr.edu/admissions/haider_program.html">Learn about the new Thomas Haider Program at the UCR School of Medicine</a>.</li> 
      <li><strong>Division of Life Sciences</strong><br />Under the College of Natural and Agricultural Sciences, the division oversees the Departments of <a href="http://www.plantbiology.ucr.edu/">Botany and Plant Science</a>, <a href="http://cbns.ucr.edu/">Cell Biology and Neuroscience</a>, <a href="http://www.biochemistry.ucr.edu/">Biochemistry</a>, and <a href="http://www.biology.ucr.edu/">Biology</a>.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://www.graduate.ucr.edu/">Graduate Division</a></strong><br />An inter-college unit that oversees all of UC Riverside’s post-graduate programs and students.</li> 
      <li><strong>Division of Physical and Mathematical Sciences</strong><br />Under the College of Natural and Agricultural Sciences, the division oversees the Departments of <a href="http://www.physics.ucr.edu/">Physics and Astronomy</a>, <a href="http://www.chem.ucr.edu/">Chemistry</a>, <a href="http://www.earthscience.ucr.edu/">Earth Sciences</a>, <a href="http://math.ucr.edu/">Mathematics</a>, and <a href="http://www.statistics.ucr.edu/">Statistics</a>.</li> 
      <li><strong><a href="http://ue.ucr.edu/">Division of Undergraduate Education</a></strong><br />Provides campus-wide leadership for undergraduate education and instructional excellence. It develops student support programs to enhance the educational experience and student success through collaborations with the colleges and administrative units. It also provides instructional support programs that assist faculty in developing new approaches that enhance student learning.</li> 
     </ul> 
    </div>

     <div class="clearfix"> 
      <img alt="UCR fans cheering" src="/Images/header_OurRankings.png" class="centerImg header" /> 
      <h2 class="intro"> Standing Out</h2> 
      <h3 class="verd intro"> We rank high in what counts: academics, research, <br /> diversity, value and impact.</h3> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_4 alpha statsSection"> 
      <div> 
       <h3 class="lightBlue huge">1st</h3> 
       <p>among national universities in <a href="http://washingtonmonthly.com/college_guide/rankings_2012/national_university_rank.php">community service participation</a></p> 
      </div> 
      <div> 
       <h3 class="darkBlue huge">8th</h3> 
       <p> in the nation in <a href="http://colleges.usnews.rankingsandreviews.com/best-colleges/rankings/national-universities/campus-ethnic-diversity">diversity</a></p> 
      </div> 
      <div> 
       <h3 class="lightBlue huge">24th</h3> 
       <p> <a href="http://colleges.usnews.rankingsandreviews.com/best-colleges/rankings/national-universities/best-value">Best Value School</a> among national universities</p> 
      </div> 
      <div> 
       <h3 class="darkBlue huge">33rd</h3> 
       <p> best <a href="http://undergradbusiness.ucr.edu/">undergraduate business program</a> among national public universities</p> 
      </div> 
      <div> 
       <h3 class="lightBlue huge">46th</h3> 
       <p> overall among <a href="http://colleges.usnews.rankingsandreviews.com/best-colleges/rankings/national-universities/top-public/page+2">national public universities</a> </p> 
      </div> 
      <div></div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_8 omega"> 
      <div class="genericBody version1"> 
       <h3> We Beat Harvard</h3> 
       <p> We ranked 2nd&nbsp;in the nation in contributing to the public good (<a href="http://www.washingtonmonthly.com/college_guide/rankings_2013/national_university_rank.php" title="external site: Washington Monthly">Washington Monthly, 2013</a>) based on our social mobility (recruiting and graduating low-income students), research (producing cutting-edge scholarship and PhDs) and service (encouraging students to give back to their country). Harvard ranked 8th. </p> 
       <h3> 29th in Scientific Impact and Collaboration</h3> 
       <p> The Leiden Ranking is based on distinguished scientific impact and collaboration. We ranked 29th out of 500 top universities worldwide (<a href="http://www.leidenranking.com/ranking.aspx" title="external site:">Leiden University, 2011)</a>. </p> 
       <h3> Most Intelligent City in the World</h3> 
       <p> In 2012, global think tank Intelligent Community Forum named Riverside its&nbsp;<a href="http://www.intelligentcommunity.org/index.php?src=news&amp;refno=722&amp;category=Awards&amp;prid=722">“Intelligent Community of the Year,”</a> marking the first time in 10 years a US city has won this award. The award honors communities that set a global standard for overcoming challenges and using technology to build prosperity and inclusion. </p> 
       <h3> LGBT-friendly</h3> 
       <p>UCR made Campus Pride’s 2012 <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2012/08/20/lgbt-friendly-colleges-universities-campus-pride_n_1813404.html#slide=1403620">&quot;Top 25 LGBT-Friendly List&quot;</a> and its <a href="http://www.advocate.com/politics/transgender/2012/08/15/top-10-trans-friendly-colleges-and-universities?page=0,5" target="_blank">&quot;Top 10 Trans-Friendly Colleges and Universities&quot;</a> list. That's out of the nearly 340 colleges and universities ranked by the <a href="http://www.campusclimateindex.org/">Campus Pride Index</a>. </p> 
       <h3> Military-friendly</h3> 
       <p> GI Jobs Magazine named UCR a <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/6766">2013 &quot;Military Friendly School,&quot;</a><a href="http://www.militaryfriendlyschools.com/mfslist.aspx" title="external site: G.I. Jobs Magazine Military Friendly Schools"></a> an honor given to the top 15 percent of schools doing the most for service members and veterans as students.</p> 
       <h3> Everybody-friendly</h3> 
       <p> UC Riverside is the most diverse University of California campus and the <a href="http://colleges.usnews.rankingsandreviews.com/best-colleges/rankings/national-universities/campus-ethnic-diversity" title="external site: Washington Monthly 2012">8th most diverse university in the nation.</a> </p> 
       <p style="width: 70%; margin: 0 auto;"> <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/about/ranks.html" class="rightArrowCTA" style="position: relative; left: 10px; top: 29px;"><img src="/Images/icons/noOnePointer.gif" alt="" class="left" />See more UCR rankings.</a></p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div> 
  </div>

     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="home-image" group="Everyone" button="727" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor toolbar="IMG_ONLY" csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700" -->
      <p><img src="/images/main/home.jpg" alt=" " width="700" height="144" /></p>
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
      <div class="col23_divided"> 
       <div class="column23"> 
        <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="left" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
        <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="460" -->
        <p>As the marketing arm of the Office of Strategic Communications, we develop integrated marketing strategies to advance the university's image and reputation among its target audiences and oversee the university's brand and identity guidelines.</p> 
        <p>We work closely with Creative Design Services (CDS) to help you identify your target audience, and to promote best marketing and communication practices within the university community.</p> 
        <p>Together, we provide a full-service approach to develop an effective and unique marketing plan to meet your specific needs.</p> 
        <p>Our key areas of responsibility and services include:</p> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Advertising/Promotion/Merchandise </li> 
         <li>Banners </li> 
         <li>Campus and College/Unit Web Presence </li> 
         <li>Creative Concept Development </li> 
         <li>Graphic Identity Program </li> 
         <li>Market Research </li> 
         <li>Photography </li> 
         <li>Publications </li> 
         <li>Strategic Planning/Consultation </li> 
        </ul>
        <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
        <div id="box">
         <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/bkgrnd_top.png" alt="" width="440" height="83" /> 
         <h3 class="accessibility">An integrated Approach Office of Strategic Communications</h3> 
         <ul id="ul_puzzle"> 
          <li><a id="a_intro" title="Introduction" href="#div_intro"></a></li> 
          <li><a id="a_cds" title="Creative Design Services" href="#div_cds"></a></li>

          <li><a id="a_web" title="Web Development" href="#div_web"></a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <div id="div_intro">

          <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="237" -->
          <p><strong>The departments within</strong> the Office of Strategic Communications work together to promote you and your university.</p>
          <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
         </div> 
         <div id="div_cds"> 
          <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="cds" group="Everyone" button="707" -->

          <p><strong>From conception to delivery</strong>, UCR’s award-winning in-house design team help colleges and departments produce communication projects that tell your story to the world.</p> 
          <p><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/puzzle_orange.png" alt="" width="80" height="72" /><a class="standout3" href="http://creativedesign.ucr.edu/">Visit the Creative Design Services site</a></p>

          <p><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/puzzle_purple.png" alt="" width="88" height="73" /><a class="standout3" href="http://mediarelations.ucr.edu/">Visit the Media Relations site</a></p>

        <h3><a class="img_link" href="mailto:margene.masten@ucr.edu?subject=Schedule%20a%20Consultation"><img src="/images/schedule_ttl.gif" alt="Schedule a Consultaion" width="197" height="58" /></a></h3> 
        <p>We are happy to work on a consultancy basis with colleges and departments across campus to help create an overall marketing strategy, and to offer specific guidance on communication projects. There is no cost for this service. For more information or to schedule a consultation, please call <strong>(951)&nbsp;827-5247</strong> or <a href="mailto:vicki.gomes@ucr.edu?subject=Schedule%20a%20Consultation">e-mail us</a>.</p>

    <div class="list-land" id="content"> 
     <!-- Main hero unit for a primary marketing message or call to action --> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Institutional Research and Academic Planning</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab4"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff/index.html">Staff</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="resources/index.html">Resources</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="data-reports/index.html">Data &amp; reports</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We provide information and analysis in support of university management, planning and decision-making.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>Our mission is to provide timely, accurate and reliable information about the university and its external environment. We accomplish this with research, analysis and reporting, data quality assurance, environmental scanning, accountability reporting, and leadership in institutional research. To learn more, see our <a href="service-menu.html">service menu</a>.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> Pamela Brown </p> 
         <p>Vice President</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/irap-org-chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> <a href="data-reports/uc-data/index.html">Resources</a> </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="http://data.universityofcalifornia.edu/">UC InfoCenter</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="http://accountability.universityofcalifornia.edu/">Accountability report</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="resources/index.html">Campus Institutional Research</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="service-menu.html">Service menu</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> <a href="data-reports/index.html">Key reports</a> </h2>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
